                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left Pend-20" style="width:305px;max-width:305px;">
                     <h1 class="Font-A-6-110 title W-100" id="article-aft-title-cosby-accuser-says-she-blacked-2-days-comedian-025336107">
                      New Cosby Accuser Says She Blacked Out for 2 Days After Comedian Drugged Her (Video)
                     </h1>
                     <div class="attribution-component D-b W-100" id="article-aft-attribution-cosby-accuser-says-she-blacked-2-days-comedian-025336107" style="max-width:305px;">
                      <div class="author-info author-info-text-first Pt-10 W-100 Bd-t Bd-b Bdstart-0 Bdend-0">
                       <div class="GridTable W-100">
                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t provider-info">
                          <a class="provider-logo" href="http://www.thewrap.com" target="_blank">
                           <img alt="The Wrap" class="Maw-100" src="https://s.yimg.com/lo/api/res/1.2/ippKmAWyPPgFeYOkbQie_g--/YXBwaWQ9bWFnYXppbmVzO2ZpPWZpdDt3PTE1MA--/https://s.yimg.com/os/publish-images/movies/2013-09-09/f3881ede-78dc-41ad-b9f0-c1efba3f8c67_Logo_Small.jpg"/>
                          </a>
                          <div class="provider-alias C-n">
                           <a class="Font-C-2-140 Fw-b" href="http://www.thewrap.com" target="_blank">
                            The Wrap
                           </a>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                       <div class="GridTable W-100">
                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t">
                          <cite class="byline col D-b Fs-n" style="padding-bottom:15px;">
                           <span class="Font-C-2-140 Fw-n D-b">
                            Jethro Nededog
                           </span>
                           <time class="date Font-C-2-140 Fw-n D-b">
                            <span>
                             December 19, 2014
                            </span>
                           </time>
                          </cite>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-right" style="max-width:500px;">
                     <div class="text-body-wrapper W-100 Font-B-1-160">
                      <noscript>
                      </noscript>
                      <div class="text-body W-100 Font-B-1-160" id="article-aft-text-body-cosby-accuser-says-she-blacked-2-days-comedian-025336107" style="color:#222222;max-width:500px;">
                       <div class="body read-more-cut">
                        <div class="pre-cut" style="height:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;">
                         <p class="Mah-100 Maw-100 Mb-20">
                          <img alt="New Cosby Accuser Says She Blacked Out for 2 Days After Comedian Drugged Her (Video)" class="Mah-100 Maw-100 W-100" src="https://s.yimg.com/lo/api/res/1.2/cVZQfyII0syVn8R1MtzjeA--/YXBwaWQ9bWFnYXppbmVzO3c9NTAwO2ZpPWZpdA--/https://s.yimg.com/os/en_US/News/TheWrap/New_Cosby_Accuser_Says_She-ce3425e9698debeb7a88029ea0ad27fb"/>
                          <span class="Font-C-1-160 D-ib Mt-4" style="color:#777;">
                           New Cosby Accuser Says She Blacked Out for 2 Days After Comedian Drugged Her (Video)
                          </span>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <iframe data-src="//www.youtube.com/embed/TH9PzkHbtMA" frameborder="0" height="400" width="640">
                          </iframe>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Yet another woman has come forward to accuse
                          <a class="autotagged group-1" data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.thewrap.com/tag/bill_cosby/" target="_blank" title="See all Bill Cosby">
                           Bill Cosby
                          </a>
                          of drugging and possibly taking advantage of her.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          On an episode of Dr. Phil airing on Friday, the talk show had seven of Cosbys accusers for guests, including a woman who was identified only as Lisa who said that she was drugged by the famous comedian more than two decades ago.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Lisa had built a friendship with Cosby after being called to audition for him when she was a model in the 1980s.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          I was very excited to go and see him, Lisa told Dr. Phil. I was starstruck. I felt invincible. I couldnt believe that he wanted to see me.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           See photos:
                          </strong>
                          <a class="also-read-counter" data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.thewrap.com/bill-cosby-new-sitcom-10-tv-dads-second-chances/" target="_blank">
                           Bill Cosbys NBC Sitcom Is Dead: 10 Other TV Dads Who Adopted a New Family
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          She said the famous comedian was respectful and kind. On another visit, he allowed Lisa, 21 years old at the time, to bring her mother and sister along.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          My mother trusted Bill completely, she said. I trusted him like I trusted my own father.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          That allegedly changed when she visited Cosby at his hotel suite for a career mentoring session. She said he gave her two drinks despite her refusals, which he insisted would help her acting.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          I noticed myself getting a little dizzy, she said. Bill had sat down on the edge of the couch. He said, Come over here and have a seat. And he had his legs open and when I sat down, I was sitting down in between his legs with my back to his crotch. And he started to stroke my hair back in a petting motion like this. The last thing I remember is just feeling the strokes on my head. After that, I dont remember anything else.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Also read:
                          </strong>
                          <a class="also-read-counter" data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.thewrap.com/bill-cosby-attorney-blasts-msnbcs-michael-eric-dyson-as-mean-spirited-reckless-video/" target="_blank">
                           Bill Cosby Attorney Blasts MSNBCs Michael Eric Dyson as Mean-Spirited, Reckless (Video)
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Lisa said she didnt remember anything until waking up back at home two days later.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          The new accuser joins
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.thewrap.com/19-bill-cosby-accusers-complete-breakdown-of-the-allegations-so-far/" target="_blank" title="23 Bill Cosby Accusers: Complete Breakdown of the Allegations">
                           more than 20 other women
                          </a>
                          who have said that Cosby drugged and sexually assaulted them. They include former supermodels Beverly Johnson and Janice Dickinson.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          In recent days,
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.thewrap.com/bill-cosbys-cousin-to-accusers-why-didnt-you-talk-to-a-lawyer-30-years-ago-video/" target="_blank" title="Bill Cosbys Cousin to Accusers: Why Didnt You Talk to a Lawyer 30 Years Ago? (Video)">
                           Cosbys family had been rallying around him
                          </a>
                          , including his wife and daughter.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          As a result of the allegations, Cosbys
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.thewrap.com/netflix-pulls-bill-cosby-comedy-special-report/" target="_blank" title="Netflix Pulls Bill Cosby Comedy Special">
                           comedy project with NBC was killed and Netflix pulled a stand-up special
                          </a>
                          it had planned to premiere on Thanksgiving. Additionally, dozens of performances on his current standup tour
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.thewrap.com/the-cost-of-bill-cosby-allegations-long-list-of-canceled-shows-and-theaters-still-sticking-by-him/" target="_blank" title="The Cost of Bill Cosby Allegations: Long List of Canceled Shows and Theaters Still Sticking by Him">
                           have been canceled
                          </a>
                          .
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           See video:
                          </strong>
                          <a class="also-read-counter" data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.thewrap.com/bill-cosbys-cousin-to-accusers-why-didnt-you-talk-to-a-lawyer-30-years-ago-video/" target="_blank">
                           Bill Cosbys Cousin to Accusers: Why Didnt You Talk to a Lawyer 30 Years Ago?
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Cosby previously defended his refusal to comment, telling Florida Today in November, I know people are tired of me not saying anything, but a guy doesnt have to answer to innuendos. People should fact check. People shouldnt have to go through that and shouldnt answer to innuendos.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          In the wake of the mounting allegations, attorney Marty Singer previously released a statement saying: The new, never-before-heard claims from women who have come forward in the past two weeks with unsubstantiated, fantastical stories about things they say occurred 30, 40, or even 50 years ago have escalated far past the point of absurdity.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:a9ae2b56-0492-311f-b248-d12325176749;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TH9PzkHbtMA" target="_blank">
                           Watch Lisas interview on Dr. Phil.
                          </a>
                         </p>
